	function acpConfig(acp) {
        acp.setMinLength(2);
        // suggestions will start when second character is typed
        acp.setDelay(300);
        //Handles click action
        acp.addSuggestionHandler({
            onSuggestion: function (suggestion, feed, metadata) {
                if (suggestion) {
                    //You can redirect to brand or category url if provided in catalog export
                    if (typeof metadata.url != "undefined") document.location.href = metadata.url;
                    //Alternatively can use metadata.id to fetch url in your database
                    //In the end, you can simply submit search form
                    else document.getElementById('searchForm').submit();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function adjustAutocompletionUrl (id) {
		var initialUrl = $('#' + id).attr('rel');
		var lastSlashIndex = initialUrl.lastIndexOf("/");
		var firstPartUrl = initialUrl.substring(0, lastSlashIndex + 1);
		var secondPartUrl = initialUrl.substring(lastSlashIndex + 1, initialUrl.length);
		var secondPartUrl = secondPartUrl.substring(secondPartUrl.indexOf("-") + 1, secondPartUrl.length);
		window.location.href = firstPartUrl + secondPartUrl;
	}
    function autoSuggestProductLink(link){
    	document.location.href = '/p/' + $(link).attr('afs-idproduct');
        return false;
    }
    
    function autoSuggestSearchQuery (link){
    	var searchQuery = "/recherche-conforama/" + ($(link).attr('rel')).replace(/<(?:.|\n)*?>/gm, '');
    	window.location.href = searchQuery;
    }
</script>

		<script>
			function tagCommanderEvent(elt, label, clickEvent, clickS2, clickType) {
				try {
					if (label == '')  {
						return true;
					}
					return tc_events_11(elt, 'CLICK', {'LABEL': label, 'XTCLICK_EVENT': clickEvent, 'XTCLICK_S2': clickS2, 'XTCLICK_TYPE': clickType});
				} catch (err) {
					/* console.log('erreur JS tagCommander: '+err); */
				}
		    }
			function tagCommanderPopin(elt, label, clickS2, pType, datas) {
				try {
					if (label)  {
						var arr = {'LABEL': label, 'XTCLICK_S2': clickS2, 'PTYPE': pType};
						for(var key in datas)
						{
							arr[key] = datas[key];
						}
						return tc_events_11(elt, 'PAGE', arr);
					}
				} catch (err) {
					/* console.log('erreur JS tagCommander: '+err); */
				}
		    }
			jQuery(document).ready(function() {
				jQuery('a[datatc-idcampagne][datatc-format],div[datatc-idcampagne][datatc-format],button[datatc-idcampagne][datatc-format]').live("click", function() {
					try {
						var idCampagne = jQuery(this).attr('datatc-idcampagne');
						var format = jQuery(this).attr('datatc-format');
						var refProduit = jQuery(this).attr('datatc-refproduit');
						if (idCampagne && format)  {
							if (refProduit) {
								return tc_events_11(this, 'AUTOPROMO', {'XTAP_TYPE': '1','XTAP_X': idCampagne, 'XTAP_Y': format, 'XTAP_Z': refProduit});
							} else {
								return tc_events_11(this, 'AUTOPROMO', {'XTAP_TYPE': '1','XTAP_X': idCampagne, 'XTAP_Y': format});
							}
					}
					} catch (err) {
						/* console.log('erreur JS tagCommander: '+err); */
					}
					
					return true;
				});
			});
		</script>

	}
}
